PTSL protocol definition file


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item See \mbox{\hyperlink{a00494_aaf8d2069e2c6bbecf4aa8f9819028e8a}{Command\+Id}} to check all available commands
\item See \mbox{\hyperlink{a02044}{Request}} struct as the payload for all requests
\item See \mbox{\hyperlink{a02056}{Response}} struct as the payload for all responses (both with/no error)
\item See {\ttfamily $<$\+COMMAND\+\_\+\+NAME$>$Request\+Body} to view actual request payload of the command (that\textquotesingle{}s stored in the Request)
\item See {\ttfamily $<$\+COMMAND\+\_\+\+NAME$>$Response\+Body} to view actual response payload of the command (that\textquotesingle{}s stored in the Response)
\item See PTSL.Send\+Grpc\+Request and \mbox{\hyperlink{a00494_aca71f39fda9a65151b32d74c7bcd4625}{PTSL.Send\+Grpc\+Streaming\+Request}} as the only RPC that operate with messages above
